| <span data-ttu-id="ebed8-1492">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ebed8-1492">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ebed8-1493">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ebed8-1493">Value</span></span> |
